ARIE 1943-1945 [vol. 063]


APPENDIX A.


A. List of copper-plates examined during the year 1943-44


ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/1 (page 7)
Placement
Mr. Ahibhūshaṇa Bhaṭṭāchārya, Benares
Dynasty
Śūra-Vamśa
King
Harirāja alias Vikramadhāma.
Date
Mahākārttika, Paurṇamāsī
Language
Sanskrit in box-headed characters
Origin
…
Edition
Epigraphia Indica
Remarks
Issued from Śāntanapura. States that the Mahāmātragaṇa with the permission of Ananta-Mahādēvī, the chief queen (of the king) and the king granted to the Brāhmaṇa Sōmasvāmin, of the Kauṇḍinya gōtra, land in the city of Āṁbrakanagara. The king Harirāja is stated to be the son of Nishṭhurarāja and grandson of [Bha]-graharāja of the Śūra-Vaṁśa. The record is in characters of about the 5-6th centur-ies. A.D. Published in J.U.P.H.S., Vol. XVIII, p. 167.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/2 (page 7)
Placement
Pandit L.P. Pandeya, Raigarh, Madhya Pradesh (findspot: Pipardula)
Dynasty
Śarabhapura chiefs
King
Narēndra
Date
3rd regnal year; Mārgaśīrsha 10
Language
Sanskrit in early (Central Indian) box-headed characters
Origin
…
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Issued from Śarabhapura. States that Rākudēva granted the village of Śarkarāpadraka in Nandapura-bhōga to Svāmiappa of the Ātrēya-gōtra and Vāja-sanēya-charaṇa.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/1 (page 8)
Placement
Śukavanēśvarasvāmin temple, Salem Town, through the Govt. Epigra-phist for India, Ootacamund
Dynasty
Western Gaṅga
King
Śrīpurusha alias Pṛithivī Koṅgaṇi Mahārāja.
Date
Śaka 693, śu. 2, Uttaraphalgunī, Friday
Language
Sanskrit in Kannaḍa characters
Origin
…
Edition
Epigraphia Indica.
Remarks
Gives the Western Gaṅga genealogy. Records the gift of four khaṇḍukas of land in the village of Komāramaṅgalam situated in Pudukaṇḍa-vishaya to the Brāhmaṇa Nīḷakaṇṭha Śarmman, the last of the five sons of Nīlakaṇṭha of the Harita-gōtra, probably by Duggamāra, the king's son, at the request of his wife Kañchiab-bā. Gives also the genealogy of Kañchi-abbā, the wife of Duggamāra, and the elder sister (?) of Indarāja, whose descent for three generations is traced from a king called Nannappa. Published in Ep. Ind., Vol. XXVII, pp. 145 ff.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/2 (page 8)
Placement
Deputy Commissioner, Bilaspur (findspot: Daikoni)
Dynasty
Kalachuris of Ratnapura
King
Pṛithvīdēva (II)
Date
Kalachuri era 890, Mārgga, ba. 11, [Sunday]
Language
Sanskrit in Nāgarī
Origin
Returned to sender
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Gives the genealogy of the king. Records the gift, by the king, of the village of Vuḍukuni-grāma together with all its in-comes to the Brāhmaṇa Vishṇu, son of Śivadāsa and grandson of Śrōttama of Vatsa-gōtra. The gift is stated to have been made on the occasion of a lunar eclipse on the day of Kārttika 15. Publi-shed in Ep. Ind., Vol. XXVIII, pp. 146 ff.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/3 (page 8)
Placement
Chief Minister, Patna State, Balan-gir, (findspot: Kalibhana)
Dynasty
Sōma-Vaṁśa
King
Trikaliṅgādhipati Mahābhavagupta Janamējaya
Date
Year 6, Phālguna, śu. di. 1, dvitīya-paksha (in words and figures)
Language
Sanskrit in Nāgarī
Origin
Returned to Patna State
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Published in I.H.Q., Vol. XX, pp. 238-244. The record is issued by the king from Aṁbarasīmapattana. States that the king granted the village of Jaṁbugrāma in Pōtā-vishaya to Bhaṭṭaputra Śrī-Gōvinda, son of Bhaṭṭaputra Koṇḍa of the Parāśara-gōtra and Vājasanēya-Mādhyandina-śākhā who had migrated from Hastipada and resided at Jaṁbugrāma.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/4 (page 8)
Placement
Do.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Trikaliṅgādhipati Mahābhavagupta Janamējeya alias Dharmakandarpa
Date
Year 34, Āśvina, ba. di. 8
Language
Sanskrit in Nāgarī
Origin
Do.
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Published in I.H.Q., Vol. XX. pp. 245 ff. The record is issued by the king from his victorious camp at Suvarṇapura. Regis-ters the gift, by the king, of the village of Kōnnapillā of Tokkārā-vishaya in Kōsala-dēśa to Kāladēśi Bhaṭṭaputra Śrī-Dēva who was a vāstavya (resident) of Saṁdākaṭaka and was the son of Gāṅgēya and grandson of Arjuna. The donee is stated to have hailed from Muktāvatī in Śrāvastī. The record also states that the donee was re-siding at Añjiligrāma.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/5 (page 9)
Placement
Mr. Babu Mukunda Das, B.L., Divan, Narasingpur State
Dynasty
Nandas of Orissa
King
Dēvānandadēva
Date
Undated
Language
Sanskrit in Nāgarī
Origin
Returned to owner.
Edition
Do.
Remarks
Incomplete. The record is full of mistakes and engraved indifferently. Seems to record the gift of the village of Dōṇōshara-grāma in Kaṇēda-khaṇḍa of Airāvaṭa-maṇḍala to certain persons by the king Dēvānandadēva. The king's genealogy is traced and among his predecessors are mentioned Vilāsatuṅga and Śivānanda[ka]. A part of the plate has been cut away and lost.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/6 (page 9)
Placement
Mr. U.V.Krishnaswami Īyer, Vil-lage Munsif, Viḍaiyūr, Tiruvallur taluk, through Mr. M.Venkatara-mayya
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
Veṅkaṭapati (I)
Date
Śaka 1523 (in words).
Language
Sanskrit in Nandi-Nāgarī
Origin
Do.
Edition
…
Remarks
Published in Ep. Ind., Vol. IV, p. 269.
ARIE/1943-1945/A/1943-44/7 (page 9)
Placement
Mr. G.Ramdas, B.A., Jeypore, Orissa
Dynasty
Nala
King
Arthapati-Bhaṭṭā-raka
Date
Year 7, Mārgaśī-rsha, Amāvāsyā.
Language
Sanskrit in box headed variety of South Indian characters
Origin
Do.
Edition
Epigraphia Indica
Remarks
Issued from Pushkarī. Records the gift of the village of Kēsēlaka-grāma by the king to Durggāryya, Raviyāryya and Ravidattāryya of the Kautsa-gōtra. The grant was written by the Rahasyādhikṛita Chu[lla].

PALNAD TALUK


ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/2 (page 10)
Placement
Ākurājupalle.--Slab lying in front of the ruined temple of Śiva.
Dynasty
Kākatīya
King
Gaṇapatidēva-Mahārāja
Date
Śaka 1[132], Pramōdūta, Pushya, ba. 1, Saturday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the grant of the village Ākarājupalle in the Pali-nāṭi-sīma for worship of god Tripurāntakadēva by Mahā-pradhāni Āreprōla Bhīma-Nāyaka for the merit of his parents Dāma-Nāyaka and Kāmasāni, and also for the prosperity of the king. Also mentions another gift by Ayalapeddiṅgāru for the merit of Pratāparudradēva-Mahārāja.

BANGANAPALE STATE


ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/4 (page 10)
Placement
Nandavaram.--Right pillar in the mukha-maṇḍapa of the Chauḍēśvarī temple.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
…
Date
Śaka 1492, Pramādi, Āshāḍha, śu. 12, Thursday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Records the resolution of the Vidvanmahājanas of Nandava-ram on the occasion when their agrahāra-village was restored to them and they were reinstated in it by Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Rāmarāju-Tirumalarājayyadēva-Mahārāja, that they would take to the study of the Vēdas and the śāstras and would abstain from levying dow-ries for marriage of girls (kanyā-śulka) in their community.
ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/5 (page 10)
Placement
Left pillar in the same temple
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1475, Khara, Māgha, [ba. 12].
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Damaged. Refers to certain honours and concessions granted to the 360 E1kāṅgavīras who were the devotees of the goddess Chauḍēśvarī by the pontiff Vīra-Śāntabhikshāvṛitti-ayya of Śrīśailam and to the grant of some varttana by the former to chākila-[Vi]rppamma.
ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/6 (page 10)
Placement
Slab fixed on the floor in the same temple.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
…
Date
Śaka 1458, Manmatha, Mār-gaśira, śu. 15.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Records that Giriyappa, the sthānapati of Salakarāju Peda-Timmarāju, constructed the eastern gōpura of the Chauḍēśvarī temple and made a gift of a palanquin to the goddess.
ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/7 (page 11)
Placement
Another slab in the same place.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1214 (wrong for 1244), Dundubhi, Śrāvaṇa, śu. 15.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
In characters of about the 16th century A.D. States that the 360--E1kāṅgavīras the devotees of the goddess Chau-ḍēśvarī invoking her aid, went to help Mahāmaṇḍalēś-vara Virūparāya-ayadēva Mahārāja, the ruler of Pānu-gallu, in order to relieve the siege laid to his fort by a certain Gururāja of Nandahāram, came out victorious and were conferred several titles by the chief in apprecia-tion of their valour and success and records an endow-ment made by them (the E1kāṅgavīras) at one rūka per head to the goddess.
ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/8 (page 11)
Placement
A third slab paved in the same place.
Dynasty

King
…
Date
Khara, Māgha, ba. 2.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Records a gift of land made by the Vidvanmahājanas of Nandavara-agrahāra to the artisans Yallā-batuḍu of Chinakoṭla and Timmā-batuḍu of Chāṁgalamaṟṟi for rendering service in the temple. Also specifies the rate of monthly wages in cash and kind to the labourers who were engaged in the work. In late characters.

ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/13 (page 11)
Placement
Broken slab lying near a private house in the village.
Dynasty
Vijayanagara
King
Sadāśivadēva Mahārāya
Date
Śaka.........., Bhādra-pada, ........
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Damaged. Seems to refer to the prohibition of taking or giving dowries in marriages among the Vidvanmahājanas of the place. Also records the gift of four villages (specified) as sarvamānya including the ubhaya-mārga-suṅkam, siddhāyam, veṭṭi-vēmulu, etc., for the maintenance of a satra by Sulire Bālayya.

Telugu

ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/16 (page 11)

Kākatīya
King
Gaṇapatidēva
Date
Śaka 11[71], Saumya, Jyēshṭha, Sunday, solar eclipse.
Language
Sanskrit in Telugu
Remarks
Mutilated. Gives the genealogy of the Kākatīyas. Regis-ters the grant of the village Chēṁbṟōlu to the Brāhmaṇa Padmanābha by the chief Vaṇaga who is said to have ruled over the Staṁbha-dēśa as a subordinate of the king. The donor's ancestry is given.

ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/28 (page 12)
Placement
Siddāpuram.--Slab lying near the ruined temple of Aṅkāḷamma.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1515, Vijaya, Śrāvaṇa, śu. 5, Sunday.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Registers the confirmation, by Siddha Bhikshāvṛitti-Ayya, of the gift of lands and incomes such as kāṇike, kappam, varttana, etc., of the temples of Nāgavarapamma, Aṅkāḷamma and Puṭṭalamma and also the right of supervision over the customary rites in these temples previously made to Guḍivāriyam Chennappa by Pedda-Ayya the former pontiff for his having built the temples of Aṅkāḷamma and later on renovated it and installed therein a new image when the temple was desecrated and the image in it broken by the Muhammadans and for having similarly substituted new ones for the old (articles) mudra, gaḍa and pāvanālu taken away by the Muhammadans, to the goddess Nāgavarapamma.

Remarks
States that the ‘Padineṉbhūmi-vāṇiya-nagarattār’, including those of Vīraśōḻanallūr and Āragaḷūr met in the Daṉmadā-vaḷan-tirukkāvaṇam in the temple of Śrī-Kailāsamuḍaiya-Nāyaṉār at Urattūr and made provision for maintaining 27 sacred lamps daily and 145 on annual festival days in the temple of Tiruvālīśvaramuḍaiya-Nāyaṉār which was thus claimed as their nagarakkāṇi. Vālikaṇḍapuram was made into a Sūradaḷam i.e., military quarter (?) and provision was also made for repairing the car (belonging to the temple) from the income of the village and the amañji due to the (officer) Vāṇavadaraiyar.

Lakshmaṇēśvaram.--Pillar in the maṇḍapa, Lakshmaṇēśvarsvāmin temple: east face.
Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1365, Śrīmukha, Āshā-ḍha śu. 10, Thursday. Irregular.
Language
Telugu
Remarks
Records that Marārinēni Rāmaniṅgāru installed the image of Parāṅkuśa in the big maṇḍapa of God Narsiṁha of Vēdādri, situated to the east of Gautamī (R. Gōdāvarī) and north of Rājamahēndravaram and granted land as sarvamānya to the deity for worship and offerings. He is stated to have purchased the land for 300 ṭaṅkas from the śrībhaṇḍāram.

ANANTAPUR DISTRICT


ANANTAPUR TALUK


ARIE/1943-1945/List of stone inscriptions copied by the office of the Government Epigraphist for India, during the year 1938-39/1938-39/75 (page 79)

King
Siddappa Nāyaka
Date
Śaka 1600, Kāḷayukti, Mārga-śira, śu. 15.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
States that on the occasion of his marriage, the chief was pleased to grant several plots of land below the tank at Kūḍligi as sarvamānya to Dēvara Haṁpeya in appreci-ation of his public services like the construction of tanks, canals, etc., and additional structures to the temple.

The donor is stated to have made the gift on the request of Chintā-Reḍḍi, Basivi-Reḍḍi, Doḍḍa Mādhava Rao and several others who were the sīmasavudars of Saṅgōji Boppa-Dēvuṅgāru.

ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/11 (page 278)
Placement
Slab set up in survey No. 1
Dynasty
Western Chālukya
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Chālukya Vikrama year 49, Krōdhi, Śrāvaṇa, śu, 11, Sunday, saṁkrānti, vyatī-pāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records a gift of one gadyāṇa by the Ugura Three-hundred of Hoṭṭiyūr for conducting the chaitra-pavitra (festival) when Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Tailapa was governing Banavāsi-12,000 and Pānuṅgal-500. Gives the eulogy of Māran of Hoṭṭiyūr who is described as a subordinate of Tailapa.
ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/12 (page 278)
Placement
Another slab in the same place
Dynasty
Do.
King
Do.
Date
Chālukya Vikrama year 1[1], Prabhava, Kārtika Puṇṇame, Sunday, saṁkrānti, vyatī-pāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Registers the gift of the tax-incomes of certain divisions and of the village Eleyahosūru by Tikkimayya, Nākimayya, Siṅgarasa and others for worship and offerings to god Bīrēśvara of Hoṭṭiyūr when Mahāmaṇḍaḷēśvara Śāntivarma was governing Banavāsi-12,000 and Hānuṁgal-500, Mahā-sāmanta Siṅgarasa was administering Hānuṁgal-500 and Daṇḍanāyaka Śrīdharayya was in charge of the pannāya tax.

ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/21 (page 279)
Placement
Slab forming part of the proper right wall of the same temple.
Dynasty
Western Chālukya
King
Pratāpachakravarti Jaga-dēkamalladēva.
Date
Śaka 1069, Prabhava, Pushya, ba. 8, Monday, Uttarāyaṇa-saṁkrānti, vyatīpāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records that the gift [not specified] made by Māṟugauṇḍa was entrusted into the hands of [Rudra śakti] Paṇḍita, a disciple of Kēdāra-guru of the Beṇṇeya-santāna, by Holliyaṇṇa for the worship of god Hollēśvara. Also records that Kūṇṭara Holla gave to Boppagauḍa, son of Māḷikabbe-gauḍi, certain lands for the repairs of the temple of Hollēśvara, when Taila was governing Pānuṅgal-500. Refers to the construction of a stone temple, a well and a maṭha by Holla.

ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions in the Bombay-Karnatak copied during the year 1943-44/1943-44/24-A (page 279)
Placement
Same slab
Dynasty
Western Chālukya
King
Bhuvanaikamalladēva
Date
Śaka 909[wrong], Virōdhikṛit, Paushya, ba.........
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Refers to the restoration of a former grant to Rudrasiṅgi-Paṇḍita by Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Āvuṇḍada Vikramā-dityadēva. Also records that the king at the request of Ballimayya, Tikkapayya and others headed by Vikramāditya, made some grants of land to the god Vibhīshaṇēśvara. Mentions Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Śāntivarma as the governor of Banavāsi. Also refers to gifts of lands made by Daṇḍanāyaka Vatsapayya, Nākayya and others to different temples.

Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45.


DHARWAR DISTRICT


BANKAPUR TALUK


ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/1 (page 283)
Placement
Andalgi.--Slab lying in the compound of Basappa Beḷagal.
Dynasty
Western Chāluk-ya.
King
Bhūlōka malladēva
Date
13th year, Kālayukta, Kārt-tika, śu. 8, Monday, Utta-rāyaṇa-saṅkrāntī
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records a grant of land by Kanaka Gavuṇḍikabbe and the Aruvattokkalu of Andaṇage for daily offerings and repairs in the temple of Hōbēśvara, constructed by Uddhara Hōbiseṭṭi when Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Tailapadēva was governing Banavāsi--12,000 and Pānuṅgal--500. Also records the gifts of toll-incomes by the 500 Baṇañjigas and the Ayvattokkalu of the same place.
ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/2 (page 283)
Placement
Hero-stone lying in the same place
Dynasty
Kadaṁba (Hān-gal).
King
Kādamba-Chakravarti Vīra-Sōvidēva.
Date
3rd year, Hēmaḷambi, Māgha, śu. 13, Monday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged and worn out. Records the death of a hero (name lost) in a cattle-raid on the village Andaṇage and seems to record a gift of land made to a person whose re-lationship with the deceased hero is not known.

Dynasty
…
King
…
Date
Chālukya Vikrama year 40, Manmatha, Monday, Utta-rāyaṇa-saṅkrānti, vyatī-pāta.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Beginning broken and lost. Registers some gifts of land by Basavagāvuṇḍa of Śemboḷal to the god Kalidēva and Basavēśvara when Tailapa was governing Banavāse-12,000 and Pānuṅgal-500 and when Basavagāvuṇḍa was the gāvuṇḍa of Śeṁboḷal.

HANGAL TALUK


ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/56 (page 288)
Placement
Yaḷavaṭṭi.--Slab set up near the temple of Mahābaḷēśvara.
Dynasty
Western Chāluk-ya.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Chālukya Vikrama year, .... Jaya, Kārtika, śu. bidige, Thursday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
States that Māḷaladēvi, daughter of Sēnabōva Rāyaṇa and Voḷajikabbe, and queen of Tribhuvanamalladēva, caused to be constructed the temple of Māḷabēśvara and that the āchārya of this temple was Sūryābharaṇa-paṇḍitadēva disciple of Varēśvara-paṇḍitadēva of the Teṅgina-maṭha at Bōdhane. It records the gift by Sūryābharaṇa, of this Māḷabēśvara and other sthānas under his charge, to Īśānaśakti-paṇḍitadēva, when Tailapa was governing Pānuṅgal-500 and when his piriya-paḍevaḷa Dēvaṇa was in charge of the manneya of Eḍevoḷal-70, Beḷvatti and Elavaṭṭi and when Bammagāvuṇḍa was administering Yaḷavaṭṭi. Also registers that Bammagāvuṇḍa and the 70 (of Elavaṭṭi) placed in the hands of Māḷaladēvi 100 gadyāṇa of gold and some lands for the same temple.
ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/57 (page 289)
Placement
Slab set up outside the temple of Rāmēś-vara.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Jagadēkamalladēva
Date
11th year, Vibha[va*], Māgha, śu. paurṇamāsye, Monday, saṅkrānti.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records a gift of land made by Mahāpradhāna, Mahāpra-chaṇḍadaṇḍanāyaka Sōvidēvarasa to the god Rāmēśvara-dēva of Elavaṭṭi. The gift was placed in the hands of Chandrabhūshaṇa-Paṇḍita. The donor is stated to be rul-ing over Hānuṅgal-500.
ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/58 (page 289)
Placement
Hero-stone set up in the compound of Gurupādappa Yaligār.
Dynasty
Do.
King
Bhūlōkamalladēva
Date
Bhūlōkamalla year 10, Rākshasa, [Kār]tika, śu.., Monday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records that a Nāyaka died fighting when Sāhaṇi Kēsi at-tacked Elavaṭṭi in the expedition of Hoyisaḷadēva against Pānuṅgal. At the time of the fight, Mallikārjuna-dēva was ruling Pānuṅgal-500.
ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/59 (page 289)
Placement
Hero-stone set up in Survey No. 74
Dynasty
Do.
King
Pratāpachakravarti Jagadē-kamalla.
Date
Regnal year 6, Rudhirōdgāri, Pausha.....
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records certain gifts of land by Tailagāvuṇḍa and the 70 people of Elavaṭṭi to a hero who died fighting. Also registers some gifts, by the mahājanas and the 1000 of Beḷvatti, of land and 10 gadyāṇa of gold for the obsequies of this hero who fought for them and died.

ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/62 (page 289)
Placement
Pedestal of a Gajalakshmī image on the sluice of the local tank.
Dynasty
Western Chāluk-ya.
King
Jayasiṅghadēva
Date
Śaka 949, Prabhava
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Refers to the construction of the sluice (tūṁbu) when Kunda was governing Banavāse-nāḍ and when Segalara Mallayya was Nārgāvuṇḍa.

MUNDARGI PETHA


ARIE/1943-1945/Stone inscriptions copied in the Bombay-Karnatak during the year 1944-45/1944-45/63 (page 289)
Placement
Ḍambaḷ.--Pillar in front of the tomb called Abdulla Vali.
Dynasty
Yādava (?)
King
Rāmadēva
Date
Śaka 1211, Sarvadhāri, Push-ya, śu. 2, Sunday.
Language
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records gift of all the toll-incomes by Saptarasa, the younger brother of Sāḷva Vīra-Chavuṇḍa, the 8 representatives of the Nāḍus and the 16 representatives of the Mahānāḍu of Dharmavoḷal to the Nagarajinālaya. Also registers gift of oil, etc., to the same temple by the ayvattokkalu and the Uguru-300.
